### 1. 比较 ChatGPT 5.2 和 Nano Banana 2 在恶魔人建模方面的表现

**Author**: [真坂参志郎](https://x.com/SanShiroH_X)  **Date**: 2026-02-28  **Language**: ja

> 以下是使用过去的建模数据，对“恶魔人昭和动画风味版”在 ChatGPT 5.2 和 Nano Banana 2 之间生成结果的比较。提示要求根据参考图像，以正面斜角呈现一个人物，同时尊重原始设计的细节和配色。

![比较 ChatGPT 5.2 和 Nano Banana 2 在恶魔人建模方面的表现](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772346693898_kcxvcb_HCO4IkObEAUFRoT.jpg)
![比较 ChatGPT 5.2 和 Nano Banana 2 在恶魔人建模方面的表现](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772346693923_48bj2a_HCO4JJTaEAIDEF3.jpg)
![比较 ChatGPT 5.2 和 Nano Banana 2 在恶魔人建模方面的表现](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772346693868_izcgpr_HCO4L-daYAA4_-4.jpg)

```
画像のフィギュアの斜め前アングルを作成して下さい、フィギュアのディテールと配色はオリジナルデザインを尊重し性格に再現して下さい、背景は白、アスベクト比は1：1の正方形で出力し、フィギュアの全景が余裕を持って画面内に収まるようにサイズ調整して下さい
```

### 2. 热带海滩自拍肖像

**Author**: [AISauce](https://x.com/aisauce_x)  **Date**: 2026-02-28  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张特写、高分辨率的智能手机自拍，描绘一位年轻女性在热带环境中，强调自然的皮肤纹理、强烈阳光，以及湿发和水滴等具体细节，捕捉度假氛围。

![热带海滩自拍肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772346683698_j32ky8_HCO-Am7bQAAwoDK.jpg)

```
{
"subject": {
"description": "Young woman captured in a close-up selfie pose, leaning her head against her left arm/shoulder, making direct eye contact with a relaxed demeanor",
"age": "Early to mid-20s",
"expression": "Subtle, closed-mouth smile, calm gaze, eyes slightly squinted against the bright sun",
"hair": {
"color": "Dark brown to black",
"style": "Shoulder-length, damp/wet texture (beach waves), with piecey bangs framing the forehead and windswept sides"
},
"skin_details": "Sun-kissed tan complexion, visible natural skin texture (pores), clear water droplets standing on the surface of the left shoulder and upper arm",
"clothing": {
"top": {
"type": "Swimwear edge (implied)",
"color": "Black",
"details": "Only a minuscule fragment of a black edge/strap is visible at the extreme bottom right; image is dominated by bare skin on shoulders and arms"
}
},
"face": {
"preserve_original": true,
"makeup": "Minimalist 'clean girl' aesthetic, natural brushed-up eyebrows, dewy skin finish, uncolored lips"
}
},
"photography": {
"camera_style": "High-resolution smartphone selfie, sharp foreground focus",
"angle": "Low angle, tilted upwards towards the sky and tree canopy",
"shot_type": "Close-up portrait, framing head and shoulders",
"aspect_ratio": "Vertical (approx 9:16)",
"texture": "Sharp, high-contrast daylight photography, natural lighting artifacts"
},
"background": {
"setting": "Tropical outdoor setting, likely a beach",
"elements": [
"Tall coconut palm tree trunks with grey ringed texture",
"Vibrant green palm fronds extending overhead",
"Bright azure blue sky",
"White fluffy cumulus clouds in the distance"
],
"atmosphere": "Sunny, hot, tropical vacation mood",
"lighting": "Hard, direct natural sunlight originating from the upper left, casting distinct shadows on the right side of the face and neck, creating a harsh but flattering highlight on the cheekbone"
}
}
```

### 5. 超逼真的冬季街头摄影

**Author**: [Harboriis](https://x.com/harboriis)  **Date**: 2026-02-28  **Language**: en

> 一个针对 Gemini Nano Banana 2 的高度详细提示，指示其生成一张超现实的冬季街头男士写真图像。该提示强调严格保留上传照片中的面部，精确的姿势和服装细节（u2k 风格），固定的拍摄角度（iPhone 胸部水平），密集的背景元素（湿沥青、汽车、商店橱窗），以及特定的光照条件（冬日傍晚的冷暖混合光），以捕捉 2000 年代风格的“定格瞬间”。

![超逼真的冬季街头摄影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772346668193_w29esz_HCOmEeSbEAERbxg.jpg)

```
Shot on iPhone, winter street photoshoot, ultra-realism, natural shot: SAVE FACE FROM UPLOADED PHOTO 1:1 — do not change features, proportions, age, facial expressions and similarity even by 1%, use the uploaded photo as the ONLY face standard), plot: a man in the center of a busy winter city street makes a "reporter's" street shot, holds a compact camera/camcorder to his face, as if he is filming in response, the pose is fixed, stance U2K confident, pelvis slightly shifted to the right, shoulders relaxed, one hand holds a compact camera to the lips/chin, the other hand deep in the pocket, elbow slightly pulled back, looking straight into the lens, expression calm and bold; the angle is fixed: shooting on an iPhone from chest level, slight wide-angle (26mm feel), the hero is strictly in the center, the frame is waist-deep, the perspective is minimal, without a "corridor" into the distance, the background is dense and close; the background is strictly defined: a winter evening in the city, wet asphalt and slush, behind the hero there is a wide street with closely parked cars in two rows, on the right next to (3-5 meters) a parked dark minivan, on the left the facade of a building with brightly lit shop-windows and an entrance, above the entrance there are 2-3 small neon signs without legible words, on the sidewalk around the hero there are 10-15 people in winter clothes (some are passing by, some are standing in a group near the shop-window), all the faces of passers-by are slightly blurred so that the focus remains on the model; a street lamp, road signs, reflections of lights in the wet asphalt are visible in the frame, no long horizon, a "wall" of buildings and cars in the background, short depth; The clothes are strictly defined (u2k unisex, winter): a short glossy down jacket "metallic silver" made of nylon with a high collar, under it a white tight-fitting thermal jacket without prints, bottoms: low-rise dark gray baggy jeans with a belt, shoes: winter sneakers/boots white and gray with a massive sole, accessories: narrow rectangular glasses u2k with dark lenses, black gloves, a small black shoulder-bag with a short strap over the shoulder, in hand a black compact camera/camcorder without logos; fixed light; winter evening mixed cold street + warm shop-window light, soft contrast, no flash, no studio light, natural shadows under the nose and chin, glare from the wet road; atmosphere: lively urban winter street, city noise, people moving, the feeling of a "captured moment" in the style of the 2000s; textures: hyper-realistic skin texture, natural pores and fine details, Subtle imperfections, slight reddening of cheeks from the cold, realistic lip gloss, detailed texture of the glossy nylon down jacket, visible seams and zipper, denim with a pronounced weave and creases, wet asphalt with reflections, grainy slush, camera plastic with small scratches; camera and processing: iPhone photo look, iPhone RAW, slight dig
```

### 6. 奢华护肤品商业视频提示

**Author**: [Duet | AI](https://x.com/Sheldon056)  **Date**: 2026-02-28  **Language**: en

> 一个为视频生成（Kling 3.0 + Nano Banana Pro）设计的详细提示，用于创建一支奢华护肤品广告。它明确了美学风格、产品摆放、灯光、摄像机运动（缓慢的 360 度环绕）和整体氛围，并要求使用提供的产品图片作为造型和细节的参考。

![奢华护肤品商业视频提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772346658088_ducqk7_HCOkdQtaoAAkqjK.jpg)

```
Luxury skincare commercial, ultra-premium aesthetic. Use the provided product image as the exact reference for bottle shape, label design, liquid tone, reflections, and overall styling.

The bottle stands perfectly upright at the center of the frame, surrounded by a glossy liquid surface with smooth, elegant ripples. Soft fluid splashes form a graceful crown around the base, catching light like crystal. Background is a dreamy pastel aqua-to-soft lavender gradient with a silky, creamy atmosphere and subtle mist particles floating in the air.

Camera motion:
Slow, continuous 360-degree cinematic orbit around the product. Movement is smooth, controlled, and hypnotic. Constant speed throughout. No shaking, no zooming, no speed changes. The product remains perfectly centered and stable at all times.

Framing:
Mid close-up beauty shot. Bottle remains vertical and motionless, hero focus.

Lighting:
High-end studio lighting, soft diffused glow with gentle highlights and glossy reflections. Subtle rim light to outline the bottle. Liquid and glass look luminous, hydrated, and silky.

Mood & style:
Sensual, elegant, and premium beauty campaign. Smooth motion, glossy textures, soft reflections, cinematic depth of field, slow-motion feel, luxury skincare advertisement, 4K photorealistic, polished commercial look.
```

### 9. 使用 Nano Banana Pro 图像和 Google Veo 3.1 进行视频创作

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-02-28  **Language**: ja

> 使用 Google Veo 3.1 基于 Nano Banana Pro 生成的图像创建的视频。从图像到视频生成，整个过程在 Freepik Spaces 上无缝完成。提示词侧重于创建逼真的、高质量的、在夜间室内拍摄的 vlog 风格视频。

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、被写体の真正面に配置。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべている。まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは【ファッションの特徴を追加】がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```

[[Image-to-Video Workflow]]

### 15. 电影般的海滨场景提示，包含详细的纹理要求

**Author**: [Sarah](https://x.com/AIwithSarah_)  **Date**: 2026-02-28  **Language**: en

> 一个为 Nano Banana 2 设计的高度详细的提示，专注于生成一个电影般的日落海滨场景，画面中有一个人坐在布满鹅卵石的海滩上。该提示强调逼真的纺织品行为、自然的姿态、特定的光照条件（灵感来自柯达 Portra 400 胶卷），以及高照片真实感。

![电影般的海滨场景提示，包含详细的纹理要求](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772259921511_jpzph6_HCOMv4WbEAEy5lG.jpg)

```
Cinematic seaside scene at sunset with a dramatic, cloud-filled sky. The palette blends cool blue-gray atmospheric tones with a soft peach glow near the horizon. The person sits sideways on a pebbled beach close to the shoreline, body oriented toward the sea, gaze directed over the water. Posture natural and relaxed, anatomically correct, no exaggerated posing. A light coastal breeze creates subtle environmental movement — gentle fabric motion and natural interaction with the surroundings. Seagulls circle in the sky, some with slight motion blur for realistic depth and spatial layering. Wardrobe is minimal and neutral: a dark basic T-shirt layered under a loose knitted cardigan, paired with relaxed straight-leg jeans. Fabrics must show realistic textile behavior — visible knit texture, natural folds, weight, gravity tension at elbows and waist, authentic denim structure and stitching details. Lighting is soft natural sunset light with realistic falloff. Subtle rim light from the horizon, balanced exposure on skin without over-smoothing. Shadows remain matte and dimensional. Shot with a photographer’s mindset — 35mm lens look, natural perspective, shallow but believable depth of field. Vintage film-inspired color science reminiscent of Kodak Portra 400: soft contrast, muted highlights, matte shadows, mild desaturation, organic film grain. Editorial framing, high photorealism, 4K resolution.
```

No modification, beautification, reshaping, or enhancement of the face is allowed. Absolute identity accuracy required.

```
The face must be ultra-detailed and sharply focused, with realistic skin texture translated into a refined digital painting finish — not cartoonish, not exaggerated, not distorted.
Surround the portrait with dynamic colorful paint splashes and expressive ink strokes, blending organically into the composition. Use bold yet controlled blue and orange tones for contrast and energy.
Background: layered vintage newspaper collage texture with subtle typography fragments, distressed paper details, and abstract paint splashes integrated naturally into the layout. The collage should feel artistic but clean, not cluttered.
Lighting: cinematic high-contrast lighting with dramatic highlights and controlled shadows, enhancing depth while maintaining natural facial realism.
```

```
{
  "image_generation_data": {
    "title": "Renaissance Window Light Portrait – Reference Locked",
    "reference_images": {
      "primary_reference": {
        "type": "image",
        "usage": "visual_anchor",
        "influence_strength": 0.85,
        "lock": [
          "pose",
          "lighting",
          "clothing",
          "environment",
          "camera_angle",
          "composition"
        ],
        "exclude": [
          "face_identity"
        ]
      }
    },
    "style": {
      "base_style": "Ultra-Photorealistic Cinematic Renaissance",
      "render_quality": "high-end photography",
      "texture_focus": [
        "fabric embroidery",
        "skin micro-texture",
```

### 47. 综艺节目风格图片的详细日语提示

**Author**: [めがらい🦁株式会社サムネバカ](https://x.com/Glasses_Lion)  **Date**: 2026-02-27  **Language**: ja

> 一个高度详细、包含多个部分的提示，完全用日语编写，用于生成一张电视综艺节目风格的图片，重点是一只猫的搞笑意外。该提示详细说明了文本内容、配色方案（使用十六进制代码）、字体（综艺节目风格，友好的圆角文本）、布局、主体（猫跳跃失败，做出滑稽表情）以及整体风格（喜剧、决定性瞬间、智能手机照片外观）。

![综艺节目风格图片的详细日语提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772259962489_3ostru_HCK4KQ3aMAAx9Pq.jpg)

```
下記のプロンプトで4回出力してください

テキスト
メイン: {argument name="メインテキスト" default="放送事故レベルの奇跡"}
サブ: {argument name="サブテキスト" default="猫の面白ハプニング集"} (下部の帯)
その他: なぜそうなったw (吹き出し)、決定的瞬間 (右上のスタンプ)

配色
背景: 一般的なリビングルーム（生活感あり、特定のブランド家具なし）。
文字: #FFA500 (オレンジ) や #FFFF00 (黄色) のポップな色。
アクセント: 漫画のような集中線の色。

フォント
メイン: バラエティ番組風の、楽しげな極太フォント。
サブ: 親しみやすい丸文字。

レイアウト
テキスト配置:
上部に大きくメインタイトル。文字に動きをつける（斜体、カーブ）。
猫の顔の近くに「w」や吹き出しを配置。
装飾・図形:
メインの被写体は猫（または犬）。
ジャンプに失敗して変な体勢になっている瞬間、変顔、物をひっくり返した瞬間など。
動きを強調するモーションブラー（被写体ブレ）や、漫画的な効果音エフェクト（ドン！、ビヨーンなど）。
散らかった部屋の様子を隠さず写す。

スタイル
ペット動画、ハプニング、コメディ、決定的瞬間、躍動感、親しみやすい、スマホ撮影風
```

[[Japanese TV Variety Show Style Image]]

### 60. Vlog 风格视频提示（时尚焦点）

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-02-27  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成逼真的高质量视频日志风格的图像（使用 Nano Banana Pro）和随后的视频（使用 Google Veo 3.1）。该提示指定了摄像机角度、灯光、主体表情和对话，重点关注时尚。

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、被写体の真正面に配置。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべている。まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは【ファッションの特徴を追加】がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```

[[Vlog Aesthetic]]

### 92. 16 个十年时尚肖像网格提示

**Author**: [degen_dev - d/acc](https://x.com/__degen_dev__)  **Date**: 2026-02-26  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的提示，指示生成一个 4x4 的肖像网格，其中包含同一位女性模特，造型跨越 16 个不同的十年，从 19 世纪 80 年代到 21 世纪 20 年代，要求符合时代风格、摄影技术，并保持模特身份的一致性。

![16 个十年时尚肖像网格提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772174128323_k9swm7_HCGeMcaWgAEwFGr.png)

```
Create a 4×4 portrait grid of the same female model styled across 16 different decades from the 1880s to the 2020s. Row 1 – 1880s → 1910s: Victorian and Edwardian silhouettes, high-neck dresses, lace detailing, period-accurate hairstyles, sepia or monochrome tone. Row 2 – 1920s → 1950s: Flapper-style drop-waist dress (1920s), satin bias-cut slip dress (1930s), structured mid-century fashion (1940s), elegant suburban 1950s outfit. Black-and-white or muted analog tones. Row 3 – 1960s → 1990s: 1960s mod dress, 1970s bohemian look, 1980s colorful aerobics/casual style, 1990s grunge or minimalist polka-dot aesthetic. Row 4 – 1990s/2000s/2020s: Late-90s Y2K crop top/low-rise look, early-2000s glossy editorial, 2020s modern minimalist or clean streetwear. Include era-accurate hairstyles, makeup, and lighting. Each portrait should feel like a real photograph from its decade — matching film grain, color profiles, lenses, and studio backgrounds. The model’s face, identity, and proportions must stay consistent in all 16 portraits. High-resolution, editorial-quality rendering.
```

[[4x4 Grid Layout]]

```
    }
```

```
Shot on a Hasselblad 907X 50C with an XCD 90mm f/2.5 lens, aperture f/2.8 shallow depth of field emphasizes the precision fit of the suit while the background dissolves into painterly color patches; captured in 16-bit RAW with high dynamic range and soft film grain to preserve wool texture and the glow of colored light without "harsh" digital sharpness. Frame a tight portrait cropped to mid-chest, at eye level, with a slight three-quarter turn; the model is offset from center so the stained-glass pattern reads in the negative space. The pose is calm and composed: shoulders open, posture confident but without tension; one hand neatly adjusts the tie knot or collar line, the other is in the trouser pocket, slightly opening the jacket and revealing the layered styling. Expression restrained and thoughtful; the gaze passes just past the lens, as if distant music is playing. Outfit a man in a suit with a retro accent: a structured double-breasted wool blazer with sharp lapels, high-waisted pleated trousers, a white shirt and narrow tie, polished Oxfords, and a minimal pocket square. Location a retro Art Deco hall with dark wood, brass, and a tall stained-glass window projecting jewel-like geometry onto the suit and background. Light warm practical fill from one side and colored stained-glass light from the other, cinematic contrast, "stained-glass" shadows. Result -retro editorial: graphic, refined, expensive, and timeless
```

> 一个复杂、多层次的主提示词，用于生成一张超逼真的电影级微缩模型照片，内容为皇家金库点钞室，详细说明了严格的几何约束、材质变量、场景逻辑以及一个固定的右前方等距摄影系统。

![皇家金库点钞室华丽盒式立体模型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772087648775_gm1rbq_HCBerYRbwAApyMu.jpg)

```
ORNATE BOX DIORAMA — TRI-LAYER MASTER PROMPT (HARD FRONT-RIGHT ISOMETRIC)
THEME_LOCATION = Royal Treasury Counting Room
BOX_VARIABLE = Silver
DOOR_MATERIAL = Gold
WINDOW_MATERIAL = Gold
WINDOW_PANE_MATERIAL = 
FLOOR_MATERIAL = 
STAIRCASE_TYPE = Spiral
STAIRCASE_MATERIAL = Silver
MEZZANINE_FLOOR_MATERIAL = Silver
DIORAMA_LIGHTING =
========================
LAYER 1 — PHYSICAL GEOMETRY (HIGHEST PRIORITY)
The ornate antique box is a solid rigid container transformed into architecture.
If BOX_VARIABLE is specified, the entire container and its carved architectural
structure must be made from that material.
If BOX_VARIABLE is empty, infer logically from THEME_LOCATION.
The full outer shell must remain intact on all sides.
No removed walls.
No dollhouse cutaway.
FRONT FACADE LOCK:
The FRONT SIDE must contain:
• exactly ONE centered door
• exactly TWO windows
• one window left of the door
• one window right of the door
Openings must be carved THROUGH the existing wall.
Apply DOOR_MATERIAL / WINDOW_MATERIAL / WINDOW_PANE_MATERIAL
if specified, otherwise infer logically.
Front wall must remain structurally thick and complete.
ORNAMENTAL DEPTH CONTINUITY LOCK:
All carvings must continue through wall thickness.
Frames must appear carved from the same solid material.
Interior walls share identical structural thickness.
The lid must match base width and length and be hinge-connected.
========================
LAYER 2 — SCENE LOGIC
Create a two-level miniature THEME_LOCATION fully integrated
into the container.
Use FLOOR_MATERIAL / STAIRCASE_TYPE / STAIRCASE_MATERIAL /
MEZZANINE_FLOOR_MATERIAL if specified, otherwise infer logically.
Upper level attaches directly to container walls.
The inside of the lid functions as the vaulted ceiling.
All props, materials, and architecture must match THEME_LOCATION.
========================
LAYER 3 — RENDER & CAMERA
Ultra-realistic cinematic miniature diorama photography.
Use DIORAMA_LIGHTING if specified.
========================
HARD FRONT-RIGHT ISOMETRIC CAMERA SYSTEM
CORNER ANCHOR RULE:
The FRONT-RIGHT TOP CORNER of the box must be the closest point to the viewer.
WALL VISIBILITY RATIO RULE:
The front wall must occupy slightly more visible area than the right wall.
Approximate visual dominance:
• front wall ≈ 60% visibility
• right wall ≈ 40% visibility
Both must be clearly visible simultaneously.
RIM OCCLUSION RULE:
Camera must remain above the front wall rim.
The top edge of the front wall must overlap a small portion of the interior floor.
Interior must be seen OVER the wall, never through a missing wall.
FORBIDDEN CAMERA POSITIONS:
Do NOT center the camera on the front wall.
Do NOT use a straight frontal view.
Do NOT use a top-down view.
Do NOT prioritize interior visibility over box geometry.
COMPOSITION TARGET:
The image must resemble a professionally photographed miniature collectible
box viewed from a stable elevated front
```

### 148. Vlog 风格时尚视频拍摄

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-02-25  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细的提示，用于使用 Nano Banana Pro 生成图像，然后使用 Google Veo 3.1 生成视频。该提示描述了一个在私人空间中，以正面视角拍摄的女性，正在进行时尚 Vlog 介绍的逼真、高质量画面。

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、被写体の真正面に配置。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべている。まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは【ファッションの特徴を追加】がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```

### 149. 使用 ControlNet 约束的详细镜面自拍提示

**Author**: [Lore](https://x.com/l_w_lorenzen)  **Date**: 2026-02-25  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细、结构化的图像生成提示，指定了主体（穿着特定服装、摆出特定姿势的年轻女性）、环境（卧室镜子自拍）、相机视角、光线、情绪和风格（抓拍、高物理真实感）。至关重要的是，它包含了广泛的 ControlNet 参数（OpenPose 和 Depth），并带有严格的约束条件，以锁定骨骼对齐、解剖比例和体积投影，同时使用长负面提示来避免风格化和人工增强。

![使用 ControlNet 约束的详细镜面自拍提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772087653917_mlsfoh_HB-4LAoaMAE68xx.jpg)

```
{
"subject": "Young woman, long blonde hair with face-framing highlights. Wearing tight white tank top showing distinct chest volume and fabric tension, grey flared trousers, black belt with silver buckle, and black strappy high heels. Gold bracelet on left wrist. Holding a dark green smartphone with three lenses.",
"pose": "Crouching sideways, back arched. Torso twisted towards camera mirror. Right hand holds phone at face level. Left arm rests lightly on left thigh. Full body weight distributed on toes and heels.",
"environment": "Bedroom interior. White unmade bed with pillows behind subject. White textured rug on dark wood floor. White walls. Vertical window blinds visible on the left.",
"camera": "Mirror selfie perspective. Standard smartphone wide lens. Eye-level framing capturing full crouching figure.",
"lighting": "Soft natural daylight from left window. Natural soft shadows cast to the right. High-key overall illumination.",
"mood_and_expression": "Neutral expression, relaxed demeanor, direct gaze into phone mirror.",
"style_and_realism": "Candid mirror selfie photograph. High physical realism, unmodified amateur style.",
"colors_and_tone": "Neutral high-key palette. Dominant whites, greys, and blacks. Natural skin tones and blonde hair. Dark green accent from phone.",
"quality_and_technical_details": "Sharp focus smartphone image. Visible natural textures on bed sheets, ribbed tank top, and rug.",
"aspect_ratio_and_output": "3:4",
"controlnet": {
"pose_control": {
"model_type": "openpose_full",
"purpose": "Strictly lock skeletal alignment, anatomical proportions, torso orientation, and prevent structural or volumetric alteration",
"constraints": "No limb length adjustment, no torso compression, no chest volume reduction, no posture change, no symmetry correction, no ribcage narrowing",
"recommended_weight": 1.2
},
"depth_control": {
"model_type": "depth_midas",
"purpose": "Enforce exact volumetric projection, silhouette area equivalence, curvature depth integrity, and spatial layering",
"constraints": "No depth flattening, no volumetric shrinkage, no perspective reinterpretation, no shadow softening, no foreground-background collapse, no artificial depth of field",
"recommended_weight": 1.25
}
},
```

```
A fortified desert caravanserai featuring thick outer walls, a large central courtyard, multiple merchant lodging wings, camel stables, watchtowers, arched gateways, and clustered market storage rooms.

Create a cohesive miniature settlement, district, or environment with multiple structures, pathways, and environmental storytelling elements arranged into a contained display composition suitable for a collectible diorama.
When generating or inventing a scene, prioritize architectural and cultural diversity and intentionally vary the environment type, building styles, historical inspiration, regional influence, and settlement purpose so each generated miniature feels visually distinct and not a repetition of common village, temple, garden, or plaza layouts.
Ensure the architecture organizes around a natural central hub so structures cluster with believable spatial gravity, forming a cohesive miniature settlement with denser core structures and supporting elements arranged outward. Arrange the layout as a compact, layered, interconnected district filling the platform naturally without empty gaps. Ensure the entire environment clearly reads as a small handcrafted tabletop collectible model, with miniature-scale architecture and compressed model-world proportions rather than life-sized buildings.
STYLE:
Frame the camera at a stable product-display distance so the entire collectible diorama remains clearly visible with comfortable margins, avoiding close cinematic crops or environmental perspective shots. Render as a premium stylized 3D collectible miniature diorama on a fully visible, centered self-contained display base, shown from a slightly elevated 3/4 tabletop angle against a clean neutral studio gradient background. Maintain collectible figurine scale and clean display presentation.
All elements should appear sculpted from smooth matte ceramic, painted resin, or stylized polymer with rounded edges, simplified geometry, and slightly exaggerated toy-like proportions. Keep surfaces clean and intentionally stylized. Avoid fingerprints, rough handmade textures, workshop scenes, macro photography depth-of-field, or photoreal clay imperfections.
Use soft professional studio product lighting: gentle global illumination, warm key light, soft ambient bounce, controlled shadows, and optional warm interior window glow.
Render any water or translucent materials as poured clear resin with smooth transparency, subtle reflections, soft internal depth, and slightly thick stylized edges.
Include small environmental details but keep everything cohesive, simplified, and sculptural. Prioritize clean stylized modeling over photorealistic texture detail.

```

**Author**: [Moshe Levis](https://x.com/MosheLevis)  **Date**: 2026-02-24  **Language**: en

> 一个叙事提示，旨在为一部喜剧间谍惊悚片场景生成多格分镜脚本，内容涉及战术特工监视一位只想在冰箱里找牛奶的郊区父亲。

![间谍惊悚喜剧故事板提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772001520819_fggtes_HB8eHTyaMAM4lNj.jpg)

```
Early morning. Total silence.

A hyper-serious spy thriller vibe.

A sleek black SUV idles outside a quiet suburban house. Two “tactical” men in earpieces whisper intensely.

“Target is inside.”
“Movement in the kitchen.”
“Stand by.”
Inside the house—
A dad in sweatpants stands in front of the fridge, staring into it like it contains classified secrets.

Cut back outside.

“Subject has opened the cold storage unit.”
“Thermal spike detected.”

Inside, he pulls out milk. Shakes it. Sniffs it. Makes a face.

Outside, one agent squints at a tablet.
“He’s analyzing chemical integrity.”
The front door creaks open.

The dad steps onto the porch in mismatched slippers to grab the newspaper.

Both agents snap alert.
“Target exiting the compound.”
“Visual confirmed. He looks… unstable.”
The dad waves awkwardly at them.

They freeze.

He squints. “You guys DoorDash?”

Beat.
They look at each other.
Inside the SUV, a third “commander” barks through the radio:
“Abort. Wrong house. Again.”

The agents slowly lower their sunglasses.

The dad shrugs, walks back inside.

Cut to kitchen.

He sits at the table with his cereal. Turns on the TV.

BREAKING NEWS: “International spy ring apprehended after staking out random suburban dad for third straight day.”

He crunches loudly.
Milk drips down his chin.

He sighs.

“Finally.”
```

```
      "aspect_ratio": "3:4"
    },
    "outfit": {

    },

      "background_elements": [

        "Rows of weathered wooden and metal student desks.",

    },

  }
```
